<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left">WATERSTONE FINANCIAL, INC.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left">WATERSTONE BANK</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left">11200 W. PLANK CT.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Contact:</font>&#160; Allan Hosack</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: right">Chief Financial Officer</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: right">414.459.4010</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-VARIANT: normal; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; FONT-STYLE: normal; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><u>allanhosack@wsbonline.com</u></div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: right">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-ALIGN: left; LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-ALIGN: left; LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt">Waterstone Financial, Inc. Announces Results of Operations for the Quarter and Six Months Ended June 30, 2015.</div>

<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 12pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN-TOP: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt">WAUWATOSA, WI &#8211; 7/24/2015 &#8211; Waterstone Financial, Inc. (NASDAQ: WSBF), holding company for WaterStone Bank, reported net income of $5.3 million for the quarter ended June 30, 2015, compared to $3.0 million for the quarter ended March 31, 2015 and $3.8 million for the quarter ended June 30, 2014. For the quarter ended June 30, 2015, net income per diluted share was $0.17 as compared to $0.09 for the quarter ended March 31, 2015 and $0.11 for the quarter ended June 30, 2014.&#160; Net income totaled $8.3 million, or $0.26 per diluted share for the six months ended June 30, 2015, compared to $5.7 million, or $0.16 per diluted share for the six months ended June 30, 2014.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt">2nd Quarter 2015 Highlights and Net Income for the Six Months Ended June 30, 2015</div>

<div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt"><br style="LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt">
</div>

<table id="4703b0b12691406ba126623e269b6593" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0">
<tr>
<td style="VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; BORDER-BOTTOM-COLOR: ; WIDTH: 5%">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Symbol, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: center; LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt">&#183;</div>
</td>
<td style="VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; BORDER-BOTTOM-COLOR: ; WIDTH: 95%">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt">Mortgage banking segment net income totaled $2.9 million for the quarter ended June 30, 2015 compared to $1.0 million for the quarter ended June 30, 2014.&#160; The quarter ended June 30, 2015 represents the fourth consecutive quarter in which the mortgage banking segment has outperformed the prior year comparative quarter.&#160; Mortgage banking operations were positively impacted by a higher volume of loans originated during the second quarter of 2015 compared to the second quarter of 2014.&#160; Loans originated for sale on the secondary market increased 26.3% to $596 million during the quarter ended June 30, 2015, compared to $472 million during the quarter ended June 30, 2014.&#160; Mortgage banking segment net income totaled $4.3 million for the six months ended June 30, 2015, compared to $1.0 million for the six months ended June 30, 2014.</div>
</td>
</tr>

<tr>
<td style="VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; BORDER-BOTTOM-COLOR: ; WIDTH: 5%">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Symbol, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: center; LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt">&#183;</div>
</td>
<td style="VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; BORDER-BOTTOM-COLOR: ; WIDTH: 95%">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt">Community banking segment net income totaled $2.4 million for the quarter ended June 30, 2015 compared to $2.8 million for the quarter ended June 30, 2014.&#160; The quarter ended June 30, 2015 included $1.1 million in writedowns to the carrying value of real estate owned, reflecting a plan to facilitate the liquidation of aged properties.&#160; The quarter ended June 30, 2014 included $440,000 in writedowns to real estate owned.&#160; Community banking segment net income totaled $4.0 million for the six months ended June 30, 2015, compared to $4.6 million for the six months ended June 30, 2014.</div>
</td>
</tr>

<tr>
<td style="VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; BORDER-BOTTOM-COLOR: ; WIDTH: 5%">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Symbol, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: center; LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt">&#183;</div>
</td>
<td style="VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; BORDER-BOTTOM-COLOR: ; WIDTH: 95%">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt">Total non-performing assets decreased $9.5 million, or 18.1%, to $43.0 million at June 30, 2015 from $52.6 million at March 31, 2015 and decreased $25.1 million, or 36.8%, from $68.1 million at June 30, 2014.</div>
</td>
</tr>

<tr>
<td style="VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; BORDER-BOTTOM-COLOR: ; WIDTH: 5%">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Symbol, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: center; LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt">&#183;</div>
</td>
<td style="VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; BORDER-BOTTOM-COLOR: ; WIDTH: 95%">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt">Past due loans decreased by $3.0 million, or 11.2%, to $23.7 million at June 30, 2015 from $26.7 million at March 31, 2015 and decreased $20.1 million, or 45.9% from $43.9 million at June 30, 2014.&#160; Loans past due less than 90 days decreased by $1.1 million, or 16.1%, to $5.6 million at June 30, 2015 from $6.7 million at March 31, 2015 and decreased $11.7 million, or 67.7%, from $17.4 million at June 30, 2014.</div>
</td>
</tr>

<tr>
<td style="VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; BORDER-BOTTOM-COLOR: ; WIDTH: 5%">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Symbol, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: center; LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt">&#183;</div>
</td>
<td style="VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; BORDER-BOTTOM-COLOR: ; WIDTH: 95%">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt">Total loans receivable increased $29.8 million, or 2.8%, to $1.09 billion at June 30, 2015 from $1.06 billion at March 31, 2015.</div>
</td>
</tr>

<tr>
<td style="VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; BORDER-BOTTOM-COLOR: ; WIDTH: 5%">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Symbol, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: center; LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt">&#183;</div>
</td>
<td style="VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; BORDER-BOTTOM-COLOR: ; WIDTH: 95%">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt">Continued a share purchase program, under which 3,895,015 shares were repurchased at an average price of $12.89 per share on the open market during the quarter ended June 30, 2015.</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>

<div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt"><br style="LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt">
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; TEXT-ALIGN: left; LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt">"The momentum of our Mortgage Banking growth continued into the second quarter wherein the division originated a record number of new purchase loans," said Douglas Gordon, President and Chief Executive Officer of the Company.&#160; &#160;"Loan growth in our Banking segment was also very strong and nonperforming assets continue to decline, strengthening our balance sheet."</div>

<div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt"><br style="LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt">
</div>

<div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt"><br style="LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt">
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt">About Waterstone Financial, Inc.</div>

<div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt"><br style="LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt">
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; TEXT-ALIGN: left; LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">Waterstone Financial, Inc. (NASDAQ: WSBF) is a single-bank, holding company headquartered in Wauwatosa, WI.&#160; With $</font>1.7 <font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">billion in assets at June 30, 2015, Waterstone has nine community bank branches in the metropolitan Milwaukee market, a loan production office in Minneapolis, Minnesota, and mortgage banking offices in seventeen states around the country.&#160; Additional financial detail related to WaterStone Bank, SSB can be found on the FDIC web site (</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif">www.fdic.gov</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">) under the "Industry Analysis" tab.</font></div>

<div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt"><br style="LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt">
</div>

<div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt"><br style="LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt">

<div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt"><br style="LINE-HEIGHT: 12.55pt">

Risk Factors in Waterstone's most recent Annual Report on Form&#160; 10-K and as may be described from time to time in Waterstone's subsequent SEC filings, which factors are incorporated herein by reference. &#160;Readers are cautioned not to place undue reliance on these forward-looking statements, which reflect only Waterstone's belief as of the date of this press release.</div>
